 say, pretends reasoning.

chapter x. power, worth, dignity, honour worthiness
 



power
 
power man, (to take universally,) present means,
 obtain future apparent good. either originall, or
 instrumentall.
 
naturall power, eminence faculties body, mind: as
 extraordinary strength, forme, prudence, arts, eloquence, liberality,
 nobility. instrumentall powers, acquired these, or
 fortune, means instruments acquire more: riches,
 reputation, friends, secret working god, men call
 good luck. nature power, point, like fame,
 increasing proceeds; like motion heavy bodies, the
 go, make still hast.
 
greatest humane powers, compounded powers
 men, united consent, one person, naturall, civill, that
 use powers depending will; the
 power common-wealth: depending wills particular;
 power faction, divers factions leagued.
 therefore servants, power; friends, power: for
 strengths united.
 
also riches joyned liberality, power; procureth
 friends, servants: without liberality, so; case
 defend not; expose men envy, prey.
 
reputation power, power; draweth adhaerance
 need protection.
 
reputation love mans country, (called popularity,) the
 reason.
 
also, quality soever maketh man beloved, feared many; or
 reputation quality, power; means have
 assistance, service many.
 
good successe power; maketh reputation wisdome, good
 fortune; makes men either feare him, rely him.
 
affability men already power, encrease power; it
 gaineth love.
 
reputation prudence conduct peace war, power; because
 prudent men, commit government selves, willingly
 others.
 
nobility power, places, onely common-wealths,
 priviledges: priviledges consisteth their
 power.
 
eloquence power; seeming prudence.
 
forme power; promise good, recommendeth men to
 favour women strangers.
 
sciences, small power; eminent; therefore, not
 acknowledged man; all, few; them, but
 things. science nature, none can understand
 be, good measure attayned it.
 
arts publique use, fortification, making engines, other
 instruments war; conferre defence, victory,
 power; though true mother them, science, namely the
 mathematiques; yet, brought light, hand
 artificer, esteemed (the midwife passing vulgar
 mother,) issue.
 



worth
 
value, worth man, things, price;
 say, much given use power:
 therefore absolute; thing dependant need and
 judgement another. able conductor souldiers, great price
 time war present, imminent; peace so. learned and
 uncorrupt judge, much worth time peace; much in
 war. things, men, seller, buyer
 determines price. let man (as men do,) rate as
 highest value can; yet true value is
 esteemed others.
 
manifestation value set one another, is
 commonly called honouring, dishonouring. value man high
 rate, honour him; low rate, dishonour him. high,
 low, case, understood comparison rate
 man setteth himselfe.
 



dignity
 
publique worth man, value set the
 common-wealth, men commonly call dignity. value
 common-wealth, understood, offices command,
 judicature, publike employment; names titles, introduced for
 distinction value.
 



honour dishonour
 
pray another, ayde kind, honour; signe
 opinion power help; difficult ayde
 is, honour.
 
obey, honour; man obeyes them, think
 power help, hurt them. consequently disobey, to
 dishonour.
 
give great gifts man, honour him; ’tis buying
 protection, acknowledging power. give little gifts, to
 dishonour; almes, signifies opinion the
 need small helps. sedulous promoting anothers good; also
 flatter, honour; signe seek protection ayde. to
 neglect, dishonour.
 
give way, place another, commodity, honour; being
 confession greater power. arrogate, dishonour.
 
shew signe love, feare another, honour; both
 love, feare, value. contemne, lesse love or
 feare expects, dishonour; ’tis undervaluing.
 
praise, magnifie, call happy, honour; nothing but
 goodnesse, power, felicity valued. revile, mock, pitty, is
 dishonour.
 
speak another consideration, appear with
 decency, humility, honour him; signes fear offend.
 speak rashly, anything obscenely, slovenly,
 impudently, dishonour.
 
believe, trust, rely another, honour him; signe of
 opinion vertue power. distrust, believe, to
 dishonour.
 
hearken mans counsell, discourse kind soever, to
 honour; signe think wise, eloquent, witty. sleep,
 go forth, talk while, dishonour.
 
things another, takes signes honour, or
 law custome makes so, honour; approving
 honour done others, acknowledgeth power others
 acknowledge. refuse them, dishonour.
 
agree opinion, honour; signe approving
 judgement, wisdome. dissent, dishonour; upbraiding
 errour; (if dissent many things) folly.
 
imitate, honour; vehemently approve. imitate
 ones enemy, dishonour.
 
honour another honours, honour him; signe of
 approbation judgement. honour enemies, dishonour
 him.
 
employ counsell, actions difficulty, honour; a
 signe opinion wisdome, power. deny employment in
 cases, seek it, dishonour.
 
wayes honouring, naturall; well within, as
 without common-wealths. common-wealths, he, that
 supreme authority, can make whatsoever please, stand
 signes honour, honours.
 
soveraigne doth honour subject, whatsoever title, office, or
 employment, action, himselfe will taken signe of
 will honour him.
 
king persia, honoured mordecay, appointed be
 conducted streets kings garment, upon one the
 kings horses, crown head, prince him,
 proclayming, "thus shall done king will honour."
 yet another king persia, another time, one that
 demanded great service, weare one kings robes, gave
 leave do; addition, weare as
 kings foole; dishonour. civill honour;
 magistracy, offices, titles; places coats, and
 scutchions painted: men honour them, many
 signes favour common-wealth; favour power.
 
honourable whatsoever possession, action, quality, argument
 signe power.
 
therefore honoured, loved, feared many, honourable;
 arguments power. honoured none, dishonourable.
 
good fortune (if lasting,) honourable; signe favour god.
 ill fortune, losses, dishonourable. riches, honourable; for
 power. poverty, dishonourable. magnanimity, liberality,
 hope, courage, confidence, honourable; proceed the
 conscience power. pusillanimity, parsimony, fear, diffidence, are
 dishonourable.
 
timely resolution, determination man do, is
 honourable; contempt small difficulties, dangers.
 irresolution, dishonourable; signe much valuing of
 little impediments, little advantages: man weighed
 things long time permits, resolves not, difference
 weight little; therefore resolve not, overvalues
 little things, pusillanimity.
 
actions, speeches, proceed, seem proceed much
 experience, science, discretion, wit, honourable; these
 powers. actions, words proceed errour, ignorance, or
 folly, dishonourable.
 
gravity, farre forth seems proceed mind employed on
 thing else, honourable; employment signe of
 power. seem proceed purpose appear grave, is
 dishonourable. gravity former, like steddinesse of
 ship laden merchandise; later, like steddinesse of
 ship ballasted sand, trash.
 
conspicuous, say, known, wealth, office,
 great actions, eminent good, honourable; signe the
 power conspicuous. contrary, obscurity, is
 dishonourable.
 
descended conspicuous parents, honourable; they
 easily attain aydes, friends ancestors. the
 contrary, descended obscure parentage, dishonourable.
 
actions proceeding equity, joyned losse, honourable;
 signes magnanimity: magnanimity signe power. the
 contrary, craft, shifting, neglect equity, dishonourable.
 
alter case honour, whether action (so great
 difficult, consequently signe much power,) just or
 unjust: honour consisteth onely opinion power. therefore
 ancient heathen thinke dishonoured, greatly
 honoured gods, introduced poems, committing
 rapes, thefts, great, unjust, unclean acts: much
 nothing much celebrated jupiter, adulteries; nor
 mercury, frauds, thefts: whose praises, hymne
 homer, greatest this, born morning, had
 invented musique noon, night, stolen away cattell of
 appollo, herdsmen.
 
also amongst men, till constituted great common-wealths,
 thought dishonour pyrate, high-way theefe; but
 rather lawfull trade, onely amongst greeks, also amongst
 nations; manifest histories antient time. and
 day, part world, private duels are, alwayes
 will honourable, though unlawfull, till time shall be
 honour ordained refuse, ignominy make
 challenge. duels also many times effects courage; the
 ground courage alwayes strength skill, power; though
 part effects rash speaking, fear of
 dishonour, one, combatants; engaged rashnesse, are
 driven lists avoyd disgrace.
 
scutchions, coats armes haereditary, eminent
 priviledges, honourable; otherwise not: power consisteth
 either priviledges, riches, thing is
 equally honoured men. kind honour, commonly called
 gentry, derived antient germans. never was
 thing known, german customes unknown. it
 now use, germans inhabited. antient
 greek commanders, went war, shields painted with
 devises pleased; insomuch unpainted buckler a
 signe poverty, common souldier: transmitted the
 inheritance them. romans transmitted marks families:
 images, devises ancestors. amongst
 people asia, afrique, america, not, ever,
 thing. germans onely custome; has
 derived england, france, spain, italy, great
 numbers either ayded romans, made conquests in
 westerne parts world.
 
germany, antiently, countries, their
 beginnings, divided amongst infinite number little lords, or
 masters families, continually wars one another; those
 masters, lords, principally end might, were
 covered arms, known followers; partly ornament,
 painted armor, scutchion, coat, picture
 beast, thing; also put eminent visible
 mark upon crest helmets. ornament the
 armes, crest, descended inheritance children; the
 eldest pure, rest note diversity, the
 old master, say dutch, here-alt thought fit. when
 many families, joyned together, made greater monarchy, duty
 herealt, distinguish scutchions, made private office
 part. issue lords, great antient gentry;

 notes war; nothing honour, vertue military.
 afterwards, onely kings, popular common-wealths, gave divers
 manners scutchions, went forth war, returned

 observing reader, may found ancient histories, greek
 latine, make mention german nation, manners, their
 times.
 



titles honour
 
titles honour, duke, count, marquis, baron, are
 honourable; signifying value set upon soveraigne
 power common-wealth: titles, old time titles
 office, command, derived romans, the
 germans, french. dukes, latine duces, generalls war:
 counts, comites, bare generall company friendship;
 left govern defend places conquered, pacified:
 marquises, marchiones, counts governed marches, bounds
 empire. titles duke, count, marquis, came the
 empire, time constantine great, customes of
 german militia. baron, seems title gaules,
 signifies great man; kings, princes men, whom
 employed war persons; seems derived from
 vir, ber, bar, signified language the
 gaules, vir latine; thence bero, baro: such
 men called berones, barones; (in spanish) varones.
 know particularly originall titles of
 honour, may find it, done this, mr. seldens excellent
 treatise subject. processe time offices honour,
 occasion trouble, reasons good peacable government,
 turned meer titles; serving part, distinguish
 precedence, place, order subjects common-wealth: and
 men made dukes, counts, marquises, barons places, wherein
 neither possession, command: titles also, were
 devised end.
 



worthinesse fitnesse
 
worthinesse, thing different worth, value man; and
 also merit, desert; consisteth particular power,
 ability that, whereof said worthy: particular
 ability, usually named fitnesse, aptitude.
 
worthiest commander, judge, any
 charge, best fitted, qualities required the
 well discharging it; worthiest riches, qualities
 requisite well using them: qualities being
 absent, one may neverthelesse worthy man, valuable for
 thing else. again, man may worthy riches, office, and
 employment, neverthelesse, can plead right before
 another; therefore said merit deserve it. merit,
 praesupposeth right, thing deserved due promise: of
 shall say hereafter, shall speak contracts.
 



chapter xi. difference manners
 



meant manners
 
manners, mean here, decency behaviour; one man should
 salute another, man wash mouth, pick teeth
 company, points small morals; those
 qualities man-kind, concern living together peace, and
 unity. end consider, felicity life,
 consisteth repose mind satisfied. such
 finis ultimus, (utmost ayme,) summum bonum, (greatest good,) is
 spoken books old morall philosophers. can man
 live, whose desires end, he, whose senses and
 imaginations stand. felicity continuall progresse the
 desire, one object another; attaining former, being
 still way later. cause whereof is, object
 mans desire, enjoy onely, one instant time;
 assure ever, way future desire. therefore the
 voluntary actions, inclinations men, tend, the
 procuring, also assuring contented life; differ
 onely way: ariseth partly diversity passions,
 divers men; partly difference knowledge, or
 opinion one causes, produce effect desired.
 



restlesse desire power, men
 
first place, put generall inclination all
 mankind, perpetuall restlesse desire power power, that
 ceaseth onely death. cause this, alwayes man
 hopes intensive delight, already attained to; or
 content moderate power: cannot
 assure power means live well, hath present, without
 acquisition more. hence is, kings, whose power
 greatest, turn endeavours assuring home lawes,
 abroad wars: done, succeedeth new desire;
 some, fame new conquest; others, ease sensuall
 pleasure; others, admiration, flattered excellence in
 art, ability mind.
 



love contention competition
 
competition riches, honour, command, power, enclineth to
 contention, enmity, war: way one competitor, the
 attaining desire, kill, subdue, supplant, repell the
 other. particularly, competition praise, enclineth reverence of
 antiquity. men contend living, dead; these
 ascribing due, may obscure glory other.
 



civil obedience love ease
 
desire ease, sensuall delight, disposeth men obey common
 power: desires, man doth abandon protection might
 hoped industry, labour.
 



feare death wounds
 
fear death, wounds, disposeth same; same
 reason. contrary, needy men, hardy, contented their
 present condition; also, men ambitious military
 command, enclined continue causes warre; stirre up
 trouble sedition: honour military warre; nor
 hope mend ill game, causing new shuffle.
 



love arts
 
desire knowledge, arts peace, enclineth men obey common
 power: desire, containeth desire leasure; consequently
 protection power own.
 



love vertue, love praise
 
desire praise, disposeth laudable actions, please them
 whose judgement value; men contemn, contemn
 also praises. desire fame death same. though
 death, sense praise given us earth, being
 joyes, either swallowed unspeakable joyes heaven,
 extinguished extreme torments hell: yet fame
 vain; men present delight therein, foresight
 it, benefit may rebound thereby posterity:
 though now see not, yet imagine; thing is
 pleasure sense, also pleasure imagination.
 



hate, difficulty requiting great benefits
 
received one, think selves equall, greater
 benefits hope requite, disposeth counterfiet love;
 really secret hatred; puts man estate desperate
 debtor, declining sight creditor, tacitely wishes
 there, might never see more. benefits oblige; and
 obligation thraldome; ones equall, hateful. have
 received benefits one, acknowledge superiour, enclines
 love; obligation new depession: cheerfull
 acceptation, (which men call gratitude,) honour done to
 obliger, taken generally retribution. also receive
 benefits, though equall, inferiour, long hope
 requitall, disposeth love: intention receiver,
 obligation ayd, service mutuall; whence proceedeth
 emulation shall exceed benefiting; noble and
 profitable contention possible; wherein victor pleased his
 victory, revenged confessing it.
 



conscience deserving hated
 
done hurt man, can, willing expiate,
 enclineth doer hate sufferer. must expect revenge, or
 forgivenesse; hatefull.
 



promptnesse hurt, fear
 
feare oppression, disposeth man anticipate, seek ayd by
 society: way man can secure life
 liberty.
 



distrust wit
 
men distrust subtilty, tumult, sedition,
 better disposed victory, suppose wise,
 crafty. love consult, (fearing be
 circumvented,) strike first. sedition, men alwayes in
 procincts battell, hold together, use advantages of
 force, better stratagem, can proceed subtilty of
 wit.
 



vain undertaking vain-glory
 
vain-glorious men, without conscious of
 great sufficiency, delight supposing gallant men, are
 enclined onely ostentation; attempt: when
 danger difficulty appears, look nothing their
 insufficiency discovered.
 
vain-glorious men, estimate sufficiency flattery
 men, fortune precedent action, without assured
 ground hope true knowledge themselves, enclined to
 rash engaging; approach danger, difficulty, retire
 can: seeing way safety, will rather
 hazard honour, may salved excuse; their
 lives, salve sufficient.
 



ambition, opinion sufficiency
 
men strong opinion wisdome matter of
 government, disposed ambition. without publique
 employment counsell magistracy, honour wisdome is
 lost. therefore eloquent speakers enclined ambition; for
 eloquence seemeth wisdome, others
 



irresolution, great valuing small matters
 
pusillanimity disposeth men irresolution, consequently lose
 occasions, fittest opportunities action. men have
 deliberation till time action approach, not
 manifest best done, tis signe, difference of
 motives, one way other, great: therefore to
 resolve then, lose occasion weighing trifles; is
 pusillanimity.
 
frugality,(though poor men vertue,) maketh man unapt atchieve
 actions, require strength many men once: it
 weakeneth endeavour, nourished kept vigor by
 reward.
 
confidence others ignorance marks wisdome and
 kindnesse eloquence, flattery, disposeth men confide them
 it; former seeming wisdome, later seeming
 kindnesse. adde military reputation, disposeth men to
 adhaere, subject men them. two
 former, given caution danger him; later
 gives caution danger others.
 



ignorance naturall causes
 
want science, is, ignorance causes, disposeth, rather
 constraineth man rely advise, authority others. for
 men truth concernes, rely own,
 must rely opinion other, think wiser than
 themselves, see deceive them.
 



want understanding
 
ignorance signification words; is, want of
 understanding, disposeth men take trust, onely truth they
 know not; also errors; more, non-sense them
 trust: neither error, non-sense, can without perfect
 understanding words, detected.
 
proceedeth, men give different names, one and
 thing, difference passions: that
 approve private opinion, call opinion; mislike it,
 haeresie: yet haeresie signifies private opinion; but
 onely greater tincture choler.
 
also proceedeth, men distinguish, without
 study great understanding, one action many men, many
 actions one multitude; example, one action of
 senators rome killing catiline, many actions a
 number senators killing caesar; therefore disposed take
 action people, multitude actions done
 multitude men, led perhaps perswasion one.
 
adhaerence custome, ignorance nature right wrong
 ignorance causes, originall constitution right, equity,
 law, justice, disposeth man make custome example rule
 actions; manner, think unjust it
 hath custome punish; just, impunity and
 approbation whereof can produce example, (as lawyers
 onely use false measure justice barbarously call it) a
 precedent; like little children, rule good and
 evill manners, correction receive parents, and
 masters; save children constant rule, whereas men are
 so; grown strong, stubborn, appeale custome
 reason, reason custome, serves turn; receding
 custome interest requires it, setting themselves
 reason, oft reason them: cause,
 doctrine right wrong, perpetually disputed, by
 pen sword: whereas doctrine lines, figures, is
 so; men care not, subject truth, thing
 crosses mans ambition, profit, lust. doubt not, if
 thing contrary mans right dominion, the
 interest men dominion, three angles triangle
 equall two angles square; doctrine have
 been, disputed, yet burning books geometry,
 suppressed, farre concerned able.
 
adhaerence private men, ignorance causes peace
 ignorance remote causes, disposeth men attribute events, to
 causes immediate, instrumentall: causes
 perceive. hence comes passe, places, men that
 grieved payments publique, discharge anger upon
 publicans, say, farmers, collectors, officers
 publique revenue; adhaere find fault the
 publike government; thereby, engaged themselves
 beyond hope justification, fall also upon supreme authority, for
 feare punishment, shame receiving pardon.
 



credulity ignorance nature
 
ignorance naturall causes disposeth man credulity, as
 believe many times impossibilities: know nothing to
 contrary, may true; unable detect the
 impossibility. credulity, men love hearkened unto in
 company, disposeth lying: ignorance selfe without
 malice, able make man bothe believe lyes, tell them; and
 sometimes also invent them.
 



curiosity know, care future time
 
anxiety future time, disposeth men enquire causes
 things: knowledge them, maketh men better able to
 order present best advantage.
 



naturall religion, same
 
curiosity, love knowledge causes, draws man from
 consideration effect, seek cause; again, cause of
 cause; till necessity must come thought last, that
 cause, whereof former cause, eternall;
 men call god. impossible make profound
 enquiry naturall causes, without enclined thereby believe
 one god eternall; though idea in
 mind, answerable nature. man born blind,
 hearing men talk warming fire, brought
 warm same, may easily conceive, assure himselfe,
 somewhat there, men call fire, cause the
 heat feeles; imagine like; idea of
 mind, see it: also, visible
 things world, admirable order, man may conceive
 cause them, men call god; yet idea,
 image mind.
 
make little, enquiry naturall causes of
 things, yet feare proceeds ignorance selfe,
 hath power much good harm, are
 enclined suppose, feign unto themselves, severall kinds powers
 invisible; stand awe imaginations; time
 distresse invoke them; also time expected good
 successe, give thanks; making creatures own
 fancy, gods. means hath come passe, the
 innumerable variety fancy, men created world innumerable
 sorts gods. feare things invisible, naturall seed
 that, every one calleth religion; that
 worship, feare power otherwise do, superstition.
 
seed religion, observed many; those
 observed it, enclined thereby nourish, dresse,
 forme lawes; adde invention,
 opinion causes future events, thought they
 best able govern others, make unto the
 greatest use powers.
 


chapter xii. religion
 



religion, man onely
 
seeing signes, fruit religion, man onely;
 cause doubt, seed religion, also onely
 man; consisteth peculiar quality, least some
 eminent degree thereof, found living creatures.
 



first, desire knowing causes
 
first, peculiar nature man, inquisitive into
 causes events see, more, lesse; men so
 much, curious search causes good and
 evill fortune.
 



consideration beginning things
 
secondly, upon sight thing hath beginning, think
 also cause, determined begin, it
 did, rather sooner later.
 



observation sequell things
 
thirdly, whereas felicity beasts, enjoying
 quotidian food, ease, lusts; little, no
 foresight time come, want observation, memory
 order, consequence, dependance things see; man
 observeth one event hath produced another; remembreth in
 antecedence consequence; assure himselfe of
 true causes things, (for causes good evill fortune for
 part invisible,) supposes causes them, either such
 fancy suggesteth; trusteth authority men,
 thinks friends, wiser himselfe.
 
naturall cause religion, anxiety time come the
 two first, make anxiety. assured causes all
 things arrived hitherto, shall arrive hereafter; is
 impossible man, continually endeavoureth secure himselfe
 evill feares, procure good desireth, to
 perpetuall solicitude time come; every man,
 especially provident, estate like that
 prometheus. prometheus, (which interpreted, is, prudent
 man,) bound hill caucasus, place large prospect, where,
 eagle feeding liver, devoured day, much was
 repayred night: man, looks far him, in
 care future time, hath heart day long, gnawed by
 feare death, poverty, calamity; repose, pause
 anxiety, sleep.
 



makes fear power invisible things
 
perpetuall feare, alwayes accompanying mankind ignorance of
 causes, dark, must needs object something.
 therefore nothing seen, nothing to
 accuse, either good, evill fortune, power, agent
 invisible: sense perhaps was, old poets
 said, gods first created humane feare: spoken
 gods, (that say, many gods gentiles) is
 true. acknowledging one god eternall, infinite, and
 omnipotent, may easily derived, desire men to
 know causes naturall bodies, severall vertues, and
 operations; feare befall time to
 come. effect hee seeth come passe, reason
 next immediate cause thereof, thence cause
 cause, plonge himselfe profoundly pursuit causes;
 shall last come this, must (as even heathen
 philosophers confessed) one first mover; is, first, an
 eternall cause things; men mean name
 god: without thought fortune; solicitude
 whereof, enclines fear, hinders search the
 causes things; thereby gives occasion feigning as
 many gods, men feigne them.
 



suppose incorporeall
 
matter, substance invisible agents, fancyed;
 naturall cogitation, fall upon conceipt, but
 soule man; soule
 man, substance, appeareth dream,
 one sleepeth; looking-glasse, one awake;
 which, men knowing apparitions nothing else but
 creatures fancy, think reall, externall substances;
 therefore call ghosts; latines called imagines,
 umbrae; thought spirits, is, thin aereall bodies; and
 invisible agents, feared, bee like them; save that
 appear, vanish please. opinion such
 spirits incorporeall, immateriall, never enter the
 mind man nature; because, though men may put together words of
 contradictory signification, spirit, incorporeall; yet they
 can never imagination thing answering them:
 therefore, men meditation, arrive the
 acknowledgement one infinite, omnipotent, eternall god,
 choose rather confesse incomprehensible, their
 understanding; define nature spirit incorporeall, and
 confesse definition unintelligible: give him
 title, dogmatically, intention make divine
 nature understood; piously, honour attributes, of
 significations, remote can grossenesse bodies
 visible.
 



know way effect anything
 
then, way think invisible agents wrought
 effects; say, immediate causes used, in
 bringing things passe, men know call
 causing, (that is, almost men) rule guesse by, but
 observing, remembring seen precede like
 effect time, times before, without seeing the
 antecedent subsequent event, dependance connexion all:
 therefore like things past, expect like things to
 come; hope good evill luck, superstitiously, things that
 part causing it: athenians their
 war lepanto, demand another phormio; pompeian faction their
 warre afrique, another scipio; others done divers other
 occasions since. like manner attribute fortune a
 stander by, lucky unlucky place, words spoken, especially
 name god amongst them; charming, conjuring (the
 leiturgy witches;) insomuch believe, power turn a
 stone bread, bread man, thing, thing.
 



honour honour men
 
thirdly, worship naturally men exhibite powers
 invisible, can other, expressions reverence,
 use towards men; gifts, petitions, thanks, submission
 body, considerate addresses, sober behaviour, premeditated words,
 swearing (that is, assuring one another promises,) invoking
 them. beyond reason suggesteth nothing; leaves either to
 rest there; ceremonies, rely believe to
 wiser themselves.
 



attribute extraordinary events
 
lastly, concerning invisible powers declare men things
 shall hereafter come passe, especially concerning good
 evill fortune generall, good ill successe particular
 undertaking, men naturally stand; save using conjecture
 time come, time past, apt, onely to
 take casuall things, one two encounters, prognostiques
 like encounter ever after, also believe like
 prognostiques men, conceived good
 opinion.
 



foure things, naturall seeds religion
 
foure things, opinion ghosts, ignorance second
 causes, devotion towards men fear, taking things casuall for
 prognostiques, consisteth naturall seed religion; reason
 different fancies, judgements, passions severall men, hath
 grown ceremonies different, used one
 man, part ridiculous another.
 



made different culture
 
seeds received culture two sorts men. one sort
 they, nourished, ordered them, according to
 invention. other, done it, gods commandement, and
 direction: sorts done it, purpose make men
 relyed them, apt obedience, lawes, peace, charity,
 civill society. religion former sort, part
 humane politiques; teacheth part duty earthly kings
 require subjects. religion later sort is
 divine politiques; containeth precepts yeelded
 subjects kingdome god. former sort, all
 founders common-wealths, law-givers gentiles: of
 later sort, abraham, moses, blessed saviour; whom
 derived unto us lawes kingdome god.
 



absurd opinion gentilisme
 
part religion, consisteth opinions concerning
 nature powers invisible, almost nothing a
 name, esteemed amongst gentiles, one place or
 another, god, divell; poets feigned inanimated,
 inhabited, possessed spirit other.
 
unformed matter world, god, name chaos.
 
heaven, ocean, planets, fire, earth, winds, were
 many gods.
 
men, women, bird, crocodile, calf, dogge, snake, onion,
 leeke, deified. besides, filled almost places, with
 spirits called daemons; plains, pan, panises, satyres;
 woods, fawnes, nymphs; sea, tritons, other
 nymphs; every river, fountayn, ghost name, with
 nymphs; every house, lares, familiars; every man, his
 genius; hell, ghosts, spirituall officers, charon, cerberus,
 furies; night time, places larvae, lemures,
 ghosts men deceased, whole kingdome fayries, bugbears.
 also ascribed divinity, built temples meer accidents,
 qualities; time, night, day, peace, concord, love,
 contention, vertue, honour, health, rust, fever, like; which
 prayed for, against, prayed to, were
 ghosts names hanging heads, letting fall, or
 withholding good, evill, for, prayed. they
 invoked also wit, name muses; ignorance,
 name fortune; lust, name cupid; their
 rage, name furies; privy members name of
 priapus; attributed pollutions, incubi, succubae:
 insomuch nothing, poet introduce person
 poem, make either god, divel.
 
authors religion gentiles, observing second
 ground religion, mens ignorance causes; thereby
 aptnesse attribute fortune causes, there
 dependence apparent, took occasion obtrude their
 ignorance, stead second causes, kind second ministeriall
 gods; ascribing cause foecundity, venus; cause arts, to
 apollo; subtilty craft, mercury; tempests stormes,
 aeolus; effects, gods: insomuch was
 amongst heathen almost great variety gods, businesse.
 
worship, naturally men conceived fit bee used
 towards gods, namely oblations, prayers, thanks, rest
 formerly named; legislators gentiles added their
 images, picture, sculpture; ignorant sort,
 (that say, part, generality people,) thinking
 gods whose representation made, really included,
 housed within them, might much stand feare
 them: endowed lands, houses, officers, and
 revenues, set apart humane uses; is, consecrated,
 made holy idols; caverns, groves, woods,

 shapes, men, beasts, monsters; also the

 generation, (and onely mixing one another, propagate
 kind gods; also mixing men, women, beget
 mongrill gods, inmates heaven, bacchus, hercules,
 others;) besides, anger, revenge, passions living
 creatures, actions proceeding them, fraud, theft,
 adultery, sodomie, vice may taken effect of
 power, cause pleasure; vices, amongst men are
 taken law, rather honour.
 
lastly, prognostiques time come; naturally, but

 fragments now extant seem invention later times)

 sometimes insignificant speeches mad-men, supposed to

 astrology: sometimes hopes feares, called thumomancy,

 sometimes lineaments face; called metoposcopy;
 palmistry lines hand; casuall words, called

 comets, rare meteors, earthquakes, inundations, uncouth births, the
 like, called portenta ostenta, thought them

 easie men drawn believe thing, men have
 gotten credit them; can gentlenesse, dexterity, take
 hold fear, ignorance.

chapter xiii. naturall condition mankind,
 concerning felicity, misery
 

nature hath made men equall, faculties body, mind; as
 though bee found one man sometimes manifestly stronger
 body, quicker mind another; yet reckoned
 together, difference man, man, considerable,
 one man can thereupon claim himselfe benefit, which
 another may pretend, well he. strength body,
 weakest strength enough kill strongest, either secret
 machination, confederacy others, danger
 himselfe.
 
faculties mind, (setting aside arts grounded
 upon words, especially skill proceeding upon generall, and
 infallible rules, called science; have, few
 things; native faculty, born us; attained,
 (as prudence,) look somewhat els,) find yet greater
 equality amongst men, strength. prudence, but
 experience; equall time, equally bestowes men, those
 things equally apply unto. may perhaps make
 equality incredible, vain conceipt ones owne wisdome,
 almost men think greater degree, the
 vulgar; is, men themselves, others, by
 fame, concurring themselves, approve. the
 nature men, howsoever may acknowledge many others be
 witty, eloquent, learned; yet will hardly
 believe many wise themselves: see wit
 hand, mens distance. proveth rather men
 point equall, unequall. ordinarily a
 greater signe equall distribution thing, every
 man contented share.
 



equality proceeds diffidence
 
equality ability, ariseth equality hope attaining
 ends. therefore two men desire thing, which
 neverthelesse enjoy, become enemies; the
 way end, (which principally owne conservation, and
 sometimes delectation only,) endeavour destroy, subdue one
 other. hence comes passe, invader hath
 feare, mans single power; one plant, sow,
 build, possesse convenient seat, others may probably expected to
 come prepared forces united, dispossesse, deprive him, not
 fruit labour, also life, liberty. and
 invader like danger another.
 



diffidence warre
 
diffidence one another, way man to
 secure himselfe, reasonable, anticipation; is, force, or
 wiles, master persons men can, long, till see no
 power great enough endanger him: his
 conservation requireth, generally allowed. also there
 some, taking pleasure contemplating power in
 acts conquest, pursue farther security
 requires; others, otherwise glad ease within
 modest bounds, invasion increase power, would
 able, long time, standing defence, subsist.
 consequence, augmentation dominion men, being
 necessary mans conservation, allowed him.
 
againe, men pleasure, (but contrary great deale of
 griefe) keeping company, power able over-awe
 all. every man looketh companion value him, at
 rate sets upon himselfe: upon signes contempt,
 undervaluing, naturally endeavours, far dares (which amongst
 common power, keep quiet, far enough
 make destroy other,) extort greater value his
 contemners, dommage; others, example.
 
nature man, find three principall causes of
 quarrel. first, competition; secondly, diffidence; thirdly, glory.
 
first, maketh men invade gain; second, safety; and
 third, reputation. first use violence, make themselves
 masters mens persons, wives, children, cattell; second,
 defend them; third, trifles, word, smile, different
 opinion, signe undervalue, either direct their
 persons, reflexion kindred, friends, nation,
 profession, name.
 



civil states, alwayes warre every one every
 one
 
hereby manifest, time men live without common

whatsoever therefore consequent time warre, every man

may seem strange man, well weighed things;

may peradventure thought, never time, nor

passions incline men peace
 
passions encline men peace, feare death; desire of
