equall taxes
 
equall justice, appertaineth also equall imposition taxes;
 equality whereof dependeth equality riches, the
 equality debt, every man oweth common-wealth his
 defence. enough, man labour maintenance
 life; also fight, (if need be,) securing his
 labour. must either jewes return from
 captivity, re-edifying temple, build one hand, hold the
 sword other; else must hire others fight them. for
 impositions layd people soveraign power, are
 nothing else wages, due hold publique sword,
 defend private men exercise severall trades, callings.
 seeing benefit every one receiveth thereby, the
 enjoyment life, equally dear poor, rich; debt
 poor man oweth defend life, a
 rich man oweth defence his; saving rich, have
 service poor, may debtors onely persons,
 many more. considered, equality imposition,
 consisteth rather equality consumed, the
 riches persons consume same. reason there,
 laboureth much, sparing fruits labour,
 consumeth little, charged, living idlely,
 getteth little, spendeth gets; seeing one hath no
 protection common-wealth, other? the
 impositions, layd upon things men consume, every man
 payeth equally useth: common-wealth defrauded, by
 luxurious waste private men.

chapter xxxi. kingdome god nature
 



scope following chapters
 
condition meer nature, say, absolute liberty,
 theirs, neither soveraigns, subjects, is
 anarchy, condition warre: praecepts, men
 guided avoyd condition, lawes nature: that
 common-wealth, without soveraign power, word, without
 substance, stand: subjects owe soveraigns, simple
 obedience, things, wherein obedience repugnant
 lawes god, sufficiently proved, have
 already written. wants onely, entire knowledge civill
 duty, know lawes god. without that, man knows
 not, commanded thing civill power, whether be
 contrary law god, not: so, either much civill
 obedience, offends divine majesty, feare offending
 god, transgresses commandements common-wealth. avoyd both
 rocks, necessary know lawes divine. and
 seeing knowledge law, dependeth knowledge the
 soveraign power; shall say something followeth, the
 kingdome god.
 



subjects kingdome god
 
"god king, let earth rejoice," saith psalmist. (psal. 96. 1).
 again, "god king though nations angry; sitteth
 cherubins, though earth moved." (psal. 98. 1). whether
 men will not, must subject alwayes divine power. by
 denying existence, providence god, men may shake their
 ease, yoke. call power god, extendeth
 selfe onely man, also beasts, plants, bodies
 inanimate, name kingdome, metaphoricall use of
 word. onely properly said raigne, governs his
 subjects, word, promise rewards obey
 it, threatning punishment obey not. subjects
 therefore kingdome god, bodies inanimate, nor
 creatures irrationall; understand precepts his: nor
 atheists; believe god care actions
 mankind; acknowledge word his, hope of
 rewards, fear threatnings. therefore believe
 god governeth world, hath given praecepts, and
 propounded rewards, punishments mankind, gods subjects; all
 rest, understood enemies.
 



threefold word god, reason, revelation, prophecy
 
rule words, requires words manifestly made known;
 else lawes: nature lawes belongeth a
 sufficient, clear promulgation, may take away excuse of
 ignorance; lawes men one onely kind, that
 is, proclamation, promulgation voyce man. god
 declareth lawes three wayes; dictates naturall reason, by
 revelation, voyce man, operation of
 miracles, procureth credit rest. hence ariseth
 triple word god, rational, sensible, prophetique: which
 correspondeth triple hearing; right reason, sense supernaturall, and
 faith. sense supernaturall, consisteth revelation, or
 inspiration, universall lawes given, because

twofold kingdome god, naturall prophetique difference
 two kinds gods word, rationall, prophetique,
 may attributed god, two-fold kingdome, naturall, and

right gods soveraignty derived omnipotence right

 irresistible; reason, power

sinne cause affliction
 
question, "why evill men often prosper, good men suffer
 adversity," much disputed antient, same
 ours, "by right god dispenseth prosperities and
 adversities life;" difficulty, hath shaken
 faith, onely vulgar, philosophers, is
 more, saints, concerning divine providence. "how good," saith
 david, "is god israel upright heart; yet
 feet almost gone, treadings well-nigh slipt; was
 grieved wicked, saw ungodly prosperity."
 job, earnestly expostulate god, many
 afflictions suffered, notwithstanding righteousnesse? this
 question case job, decided god himselfe, by
 arguments derived job’s sinne, power. whereas the
 friends job drew arguments affliction sinne,
 defended himselfe conscience innocence, god
 himselfe taketh matter, justified affliction by
 arguments drawn power, "where thou i
 layd foundations earth," like, approved
 job’s innocence, reproved erroneous doctrine friends.
 conformable doctrine sentence saviour, concerning

honour worship what
 
honour consisteth inward thought, opinion power, and

 power goodnesse, possible. opinion, the

 intend honour, seem ridiculous, tending contumely; they
 worship; signe signe giveth it,

scope
 
although books written divers men, yet manifest
 writers indued one spirit, they
 conspire one end, setting forth the
 rights kingdome god, father, son, holy ghost. for
 book genesis, deriveth genealogy gods people, the
 creation world, going egypt: four books of
 moses, contain election god king, laws which
 hee prescribed government: books joshua, judges, ruth,
 samuel, time saul, describe acts gods people,
 till time cast gods yoke, called king, the
 manner neighbour nations; rest history the
 old testament, derives succession line david, the
 captivity, line spring restorer kingdome
 god, even blessed saviour god son, whose coming foretold
 bookes prophets, evangelists writt his
 life, actions, claim kingdome, whilst lived one
 earth: lastly, acts, epistles apostles, declare the
 coming god, holy ghost, authority left them, and
 successors, direction jews, invitation
 gentiles. summe, histories prophecies old
 testament, gospels, epistles new testament, had
 one scope, convert men obedience god; 1. in
 moses, priests; 2. man christ; 3. apostles and
 successors apostolicall power. three several times
 represent person god: moses, successors high
 priests, kings judah, old testament: christ himself, in
 time lived earth: apostles, successors, from
 day pentecost (when holy ghost descended them) this
 day.
 



question authority scriptures stated.
 
question much disputed divers sects christian
 religion, whence scriptures derive authority; which
 question also propounded sometimes terms, as, wee know
 word god, or, beleeve so: the
 difficulty resolving it, ariseth chiefly impropernesse of
 words wherein question self couched. beleeved
 hands, first originall author god; and
 consequently question disputed, that. again, manifest,
 none can know gods word, (though true christians
 beleeve it,) god hath revealed it
 supernaturally; therefore question rightly moved, our
 knowledge it. lastly, question propounded beleefe;
 moved beleeve one, others reasons,
 can rendred one generall answer all. question
 truly stated is, authority made law.
 



authority interpretation
 
far differ laws nature, doubt,
 law god, carry authority them,
 legible men use naturall reason: is
 authority, morall doctrine consonant to
 reason; dictates whereof laws, made, eternall.
 
made law god himselfe, nature written
 law, laws god hath sufficiently
 published them, man can excuse himself, saying, know not
 his.
 
therefore, god hath supernaturally revealed, they
 his, published them, sent him, not
 obliged obey them, authority, his, whose commands have
 already force laws; say, authority, then
 common-wealth, residing soveraign, the
 legislative power. again, legislative authority of
 common-wealth, giveth force laws, must bee
 authority derived god, either private, publique:
 private, obliges onely him, particular god hath been
 pleased reveale it. every man obliged, take for
 gods law, particular men, pretence private inspiration, or
 revelation, obtrude upon him, (in number men, out
 pride, ignorance, take dreams, extravagant fancies,
 madnesse, testimonies gods spirit; ambition,
 pretend divine testimonies, falsely, contrary their
 consciences,) impossible divine law be
 acknowledged. publique, authority common-wealth, or
 church. church, one person, thing
 common-wealth christians; called common-wealth, it
 consisteth men united one person, soveraign; church,
 consisteth christian men, united one christian
 soveraign. church one person, hath no
 authority all; can neither command, doe action all; nor
 capable power, right thing; will,
 reason, voice; qualities personall. now the
 whole number christians contained one common-wealth, they
 one person; universall church hath any
 authority them; therefore scriptures made laws,
 universall church: bee one common-wealth, all
 christian monarchs, states private persons, subject to
 bee judged, deposed, punished universall soveraigne all
 christendome. question authority scriptures is
 reduced this, "whether christian kings, soveraigne assemblies
 christian common-wealths, absolute territories,
 immediately god; subject one vicar christ, constituted
 universall church; bee judged, condemned, deposed, put
 death, hee shall think expedient, necessary common
 good."
 
question bee resolved, without particular
 consideration kingdome god; whence also, wee judge
 authority interpreting scripture. for, whosoever hath a
 lawfull power writing, make law, hath power also to
 approve, disapprove interpretation same.

chapter xxxv. signification scripture kingdome god, of

kingdom god taken divines metaphorically scriptures
 properly
 
kingdome god writings divines, specially in

creation, god reigned men naturally by

 one man speaketh another. manner reigned adam,

kingdome god properly civill soveraignty a
 peculiar people pact
 
covenant, foot mount sinai, renewed moses (exod.
 19.5.) lord commandeth moses speak people this
 manner, "if will obey voice indeed, keep covenant, then
 yee shall peculiar people me, earth mine; and
 yee shall unto sacerdotall kingdome, holy nation." a
 "peculiar people" vulgar latine hath, peculium cunctis populis:
 english translation made beginning reign king
 james, hath, "peculiar treasure unto nations;" the
 geneva french, "the precious jewel nations." truest

 (tit. 2.14.) saith, alluding place, blessed
 saviour "gave us, might purifie us himself, a

 greek periousios, opposed commonly word epiousios: and
 signifieth ordinary, quotidian, (as lords prayer) of
 daily use; signifieth overplus, stored
 up, enjoyed speciall manner; latines call peculium;
 meaning place confirmed reason god rendereth

confirmed expresse words text, "yee

again, title holy nation confirmes same: holy
 signifies, gods speciall, generall right. all

 called holy, onely set apart especiall

 one place, kingdome god, properly meant a

 lieutenant.
 
many places clearly prove same. first (1

israelites rejected god, prophets foretell his

literall interpretation kingdome god, ariseth also
 true interpretation word holy. word, in
 gods kingdome answereth that, men kingdomes use to
 call publique, kings.
 
king countrey publique person, representative of
 subjects. god king israel holy one of
 israel. nation subject one earthly soveraign, the
 nation soveraign, is, publique person. jews,
 gods nation, called (exod. 19.6.) "a holy nation." by
 holy, alwaies understood, either god himselfe, gods
 propriety; publique alwaies meant, either person the
 common-wealth self, something common-wealths, no
 private person can claim propriety therein.
 
therefore sabbath (gods day) holy day; temple, (gods house)
 holy house; sacrifices, tithes, offerings (gods tribute) holy
 duties; priests, prophets, anointed kings, christ (gods
 ministers) holy men; coelestiall ministring spirits (gods
 messengers) holy angels; like: wheresoever word holy is
 taken properly, still something signified propriety, gotten
 consent. saying "hallowed thy name," pray god for
 grace keep first commandement, "having gods but
 him." mankind gods nation propriety: jews holy
 nation. why, became propriety covenant.
 



sacred what
 
word profane, usually taken scripture same
 common; consequently contraries, holy, proper, the
 kingdome god must also. figuratively, men also
 called holy, led godly lives, forsaken all
 worldly designes, wholly devoted, given god.
 proper sense, made holy gods appropriating or
 separating use, said sanctified god, the
 seventh day fourth commandement; elect new
 testament said bee sanctified, endued the
 spirit godlinesse. made holy dedication of
 men, given god, used onely publique service,
 called also sacred, said consecrated, temples, other
 houses publique prayer, utensils, priests, ministers,
 victimes, offerings, externall matter sacraments.
 



degrees sanctity
 
holinesse degrees: things set apart
 service god, may bee set apart again, neerer
 especial service. whole nation israelites a
 people holy god; yet tribe levi amongst israelites a
 holy tribe; amongst levites, priests yet holy; and
 amongst priests, high priest holy. land
 judea holy land; holy city wherein god be
 worshipped, holy; again, temples holy the
 city; sanctum sanctorum holy rest temple.
 



sacrament
 
sacrament, separation visible thing common use;
 consecration gods service, sign, either our
 admission kingdome god, number peculiar
 people, commemoration same. old testament, the
 sign admission circumcision; new testament, baptisme. the
 commemoration old testament, eating (at certain
 time, anniversary) paschall lamb; were
 put mind night wherein delivered their
 bondage egypt; new testament, celebrating the
 lords supper; which, put mind, deliverance from
 bondage sin, blessed saviours death upon crosse. the
 sacraments admission, used, needs
 one admission; need often put in
 mind deliverance, allegeance, sacraments of
 commemoration need reiterated. principall
 sacraments, solemne oathes make our
 alleageance. also consecrations, may called
 sacraments, word implyeth onely consecration gods service; but
 implies oath, promise alleageance god, no
 old testament, circumcision, passover; nor
 new testament, baptisme, lords
 supper.

word what
 
mention word god, man, doth not
 signifie part speech, grammarians call nown, verb,

 interrogateth. sense vocabulum, signifies a
 word; sermo, (in greek logos) speech, discourse, or
 saying.

praediction future contingents, alwaies prophecy
 
prophecy meant praediction, foretelling future
 contingents; prophets, gods spokesmen, and
 foretold things others, god foretold them; but

 prophecy, one casuall event may bee wrested their

 came upon saul, prophecyed midst house."
 



manner god hath spoken prophets
 
although many significations scripture word
 prophet; yet frequent, taken him,
 god speaketh immediately, prophet say from
 him, man, people. hereupon question may
 asked, manner god speaketh prophet. can (may some
 say) properly said, god hath voice language, cannot
 properly said, hath tongue, organs, man? the
 prophet david argueth thus, "shall made eye, see? he
 made ear, hear?" may spoken, (as usually) to
 signifie gods nature, signifie intention honor him. for
 see, hear, honorable attributes, may given god, to
 declare (as far capacity can conceive) almighty power. but
 taken strict, proper sense, one might argue
 making parts mans body, also use
 have; many uncomely, it
 greatest contumely world ascribe him.
 therefore interpret gods speaking men immediately, that
 way (whatsoever be), god makes understand will: and
 wayes whereby doth this, many; sought onely the
 holy scripture: though many times said, god spake to
 this, person, without declaring manner; yet be
 many places, deliver also signes were
 acknowledge presence, commandement; may be
 understood, spake many rest.

every man examine probability pretended prophets
 calling
 
seeing prophecy supposeth vision, dream, (which two, when
 naturall, same,) especiall gift god, so
 rarely observed mankind, admired observed; seeing
 well gifts, extraordinary dreams, visions, may
 proceed god, onely supernaturall, immediate, but
 also naturall operation, mediation second causes;
 need reason judgement discern naturall, and
 supernaturall gifts, naturall, supernaturall visions, or
 dreams. consequently men need circumspect, wary,
 obeying voice man, pretending prophet,
 requires us obey god way, gods name telleth us to
 way happinesse. pretends teach men way of
 great felicity, pretends govern them; say, rule, and
 reign them; thing, men naturally desire, and
 therefore worthy suspected ambition imposture; and
 consequently, examined, tryed every man, hee
 yeeld obedience; unlesse yeelded already, in
 institution common-wealth; prophet civill
 soveraign, civil soveraign authorized. examination
 prophets, spirits, allowed every one people,
 purpose, set marks, every man
 might able, distinguish those, ought, those
 follow. seeing therefore marks set out
 (deut. 13. 1,&c.) know prophet by; (1 john 4.1.&c) know a

chapter xxxvii. miracles, use
 



miracle work causeth admiration
 
miracles signified admirable works god: & therefore they
 also called wonders. part, done,
 signification commandement, occasions, as
 without them, men apt doubt, (following private naturall
 reasoning,) hath commanded, not, commonly in
 holy scripture, called signes, sense, called by
 latines, ostenta, portenta, shewing, fore-signifying
 that, almighty bring passe.
 



must therefore rare, whereof naturall cause known
 
understand therefore miracle, must first understand what
 works are, men wonder at, call admirable. be
 two things make men wonder event: one is, it
 strange, say, such, like hath never, very
 rarely produced: is, produced, cannot
 imagine done naturall means, onely the
 immediate hand god. wee see possible, naturall cause of
 it, rarely soever like done; like been
 often done, impossible soever imagine naturall means
 thereof, wonder, esteem miracle.
 
therefore, horse, cow speak, miracle; because
 thing strange, & naturall cause difficult imagin: so
 also it, see strange deviation nature, production
 new shape living creature. man, animal,
 engenders like, though know done, the
 other; yet ’tis usuall, miracle. like manner, a
 man metamorphosed stone, pillar, miracle;
 strange: peece wood changed; see it
 often, miracle: yet know more, operation of
 god, one brought passe, other.
 
first rainbow seen world, miracle, the
 first; consequently strange; served sign god, placed
 heaven, assure people, universall
 destruction world water. day, they
 frequent, miracles, neither know their
 naturall causes, know not. again, many
 rare works produced art man: yet know done;
 thereby wee know also means done, count them
 miracles, wrought immediate hand god, but
 mediation humane industry.
 



seemeth miracle one man, may seem otherwise another
 
furthermore, seeing admiration wonder, consequent the
 knowledge experience, wherewith men endued, more, some
 lesse; followeth, thing, may miracle one, and
 another. thence is, ignorant, superstitious men
 make great wonders works, men, knowing proceed
 nature, (which immediate, ordinary work god,)
 admire all: ecclipses sun moon taken
 supernaturall works, common people; neverthelesse, there
 others, naturall causes, foretold very
 hour arrive: or, man, confederacy, secret
 intelligence, getting knowledge private actions ignorant,
 unwary man, thereby tells him, done former time; seems
 miraculous thing; amongst wise, cautelous men, such
 miracles those, easily done.
 



end miracles
 
again, belongeth nature miracle, wrought for

 prayer, word man. works god egypt,

definition miracle
 
set down, nature, use a

definition, may inferre; first, miracles,

chapter xxxix. signification scripture word church
 



church lords house
 
word church, (ecclesia) signifieth books holy scripture
 divers things. sometimes (though often) taken gods house,
 say, temple, wherein christians assemble perform
 holy duties publiquely; as, 1 cor. 14. ver. 34. "let women keep
 silence churches:" metaphorically put, the

 prayer; edifice dedicated christians worship of
 christ, christs house: therefore greek fathers call kuriake,
 lords house; thence, language came called kyrke,
 church.

church (when taken house) signifieth ecclesia
 signified grecian common-wealths; say, congregation,

 unto them; common-wealth rome called concio, as
 spake called ecclesiastes, concionator. they

 legitima, lawfull church, ennomos ecclesia. excited
 tumultuous, seditious clamor, confused church,
 ecclesia sugkechumene.
 
taken also sometimes men right the

chapter xli. office blessed saviour
 



three parts office christ
 
find holy scripture three parts office messiah: the
 first redeemer, saviour: second pastor, counsellour,
 teacher, is, prophet sent god, convert god
 hath elected salvation; third king, eternall king, but
 father, moses high priests severall

 ministers; will continue work till coming again. after
 coming again, shall begin glorious reign elect,
 last eternally.

christs kingdome world
 
much therefore, redeemeth, hath title thing

trinity
 
wee person god born now third time. moses,
 high priests, gods representative old testament;
 saviour himselfe man, abode earth: holy
 ghost, say, apostles, successors, office
 preaching, teaching, received holy spirit, have
 represented ever since. person, (as shewn before,
 [chapt. 16.].) represented, often hee is
 represented; therefore god, represented (that is,
 personated) thrice, may properly enough said three persons;
 though neither word person, trinity ascribed the
 bible. st. john indeed (1 epist. 5.7.) saith, "there three bear
 witnesse heaven, father, word, holy spirit; these
 three one:" disagreeth not, accordeth fitly three
 persons proper signification persons; is, is
 represented another. god father, represented moses,
 one person; represented sonne, another person, as
 represented apostles, doctors taught authority
 derived, third person; yet every person here, is
 person one god. man may ask, was
 whereof three bare witnesse. st. john therefore tells us (verse
 11.) bear witnesse, "god hath given us eternall life
 son." again, asked, wherein testimony
 appeareth, answer easie; hath testified the
 miracles wrought, first moses; secondly, himself; and
 lastly apostles, received holy spirit; which
 times represented person god; either prophecyed, or
 preached jesus christ. apostles, character
 apostleship, twelve first great apostles, bear
 witnesse resurrection; appeareth expressely (acts 1. ver.
 21,22.) st peter, new apostle chosen place
 judas iscariot, useth words, "of men companied
 us time lord jesus went amongst us,
 beginning baptisme john, unto day hee was
 taken us, must one bee ordained witnesse us his
 resurrection:" words interpret bearing witnesse, mentioned
 st. john. place mentioned another trinity of
 witnesses earth. (ver. 8.) saith, "there three bear
 witnesse earth, spirit, water, bloud; these
 three agree one:" say, graces gods spirit, the
 two sacraments, baptisme, lords supper, agree one
 testimony, assure consciences beleevers, eternall life; of
 testimony saith (verse 10.) "he beleeveth of
 man hath witnesse himselfe." trinity earth unity
 thing; spirit, water, bloud, not
 substance, though give testimony: the
 trinity heaven, persons persons one god,
 though represented three different times occasions. conclude,
 doctrine trinity, far can gathered directly from
 scripture, substance this; god alwaies one the
 same, person represented moses; person represented by
 incarnate; person represented apostles. as
 represented apostles, holy spirit spake, is
 god; represented (that god man), that
 god; represented moses, high priests, father, is
 say, father lord jesus christ, god: whence
 may gather reason names father, son, holy spirit in
 signification godhead, never used old testament:
 persons, is, names representing;
 be, till divers men represented gods person in
 ruling, directing him.
 
thus wee see power ecclesiasticall left saviour
 apostles; (to end might better
 exercise power,) endued holy spirit, therefore
 called sometime new testament paracletus signifieth an
 assister, one called helpe, though bee commonly translated
 comforter. let us now consider power selfe, was, and
 whom.
 



power ecclesiasticall power teach

 kingdom god comes; apostles, ministers
 gospel, schoolemasters, commanders, their
 precepts laws, wholesome counsells dispute in

nature faith:
 
again, office christs ministers world, make men

authority christ hath left civill princes
 
another argument, ministers christ present world
 right commanding, may drawn lawfull authority
 christ hath left princes, well christians, infidels.
 st. paul saith (col. 3.20.) "children obey parents things;
 well pleasing lord." ver. 22. "servants obey in

 spoken whose masters infidells; yet bidden

 sent punishment evill doers, and
 praise doe well; will god."
 st. paul (tit. 3.1.) "put men mind subject to

 much therefore obey christians, god hath
 ordained soveraign power us. can wee obliged
 doe thing contrary command king, soveraign
 representant common-wealth, whereof members, whom
 look protected? therefore manifest, christ hath not
 left ministers world, unlesse also endued with
 civill authority, authority command men.
 



christians may avoid persecution
 
(may object) king, senate, soveraign
 person forbid us beleeve christ? answer, such
 forbidding effect, beleef, unbeleef never follow
 mens commands. faith gift god, man can neither give, nor

 asked, wee bee commanded lawfull prince, say
 tongue, wee beleeve not; must obey command? profession
 tongue externall thing, other
 gesture whereby signifie obedience; wherein christian,
 holding firmely heart faith christ, hath liberty
 prophet elisha allowed naaman syrian. naaman was
 converted heart god israel; hee saith (2 kings
 5.17.) "thy servant will henceforth offer neither burnt offering, nor

 done lips. shall answer our

 father heaven?" may say, whatsoever
 subject, naaman was, compelled obedience soveraign,
 doth order mind, order laws of
 country, action his, soveraigns; he

 law countrey. man shall accuse doctrine, repugnant

 bee present divine service christian church, on

martyrs
 
shall say martyrs read the
 history church, needlessely cast away lives?
 answer hereunto, distinguish persons been
 cause put death; whereof received calling to
 preach, professe kingdome christ openly; others no
 calling, required owne faith.
 former sort, put death, bearing witnesse to
 point, jesus christ risen dead, true martyrs;
 martyr is, (to give true definition word) witnesse of
 resurrection jesus messiah; none can those
 conversed earth, saw risen: a
 witnesse must seen testifieth, else testimony not
 good. none such, can properly called martyrs christ,
 manifest words st. peter, act. 1.21, 22. "wherefore of

 must disciple conversed him, saw before, and

 disciples: whereas so, can witnesse more, but

 mens testimony; second martyrs, martyrs christs
 witnesses.
 
he, maintain every doctrine draweth of
 history saviours life, acts, epistles the

 wil oppose laws authority civill state, far from

 profit clergy, required; death the

 put death testimony, not.
 
also sent preach fundamentall article, taketh

 warrant preach christ come flesh; say,

argument points commission
 
lastly points commission, expressely set down
 gospel, contain none authority congregation.

 even man came, ministred unto, minister.

teach
 
another point commission, is, teach nations; in

 "three sabbath days reasoned scriptures,
 opening, alledging christ must needs suffered, risen
 dead, jesus christ." teach out
 old testament jesus christ, (that say, king,)
 risen dead, say, men bound they
 beleeve it, obey tell so, laws, and
 commands soveraigns; shall doe wisely, expect
 coming christ hereafter, patience, faith, obedience
 present magistrates.
 



baptize;
 
another point commission, baptize, "in name of
 father, son, holy ghost." baptisme?
 dipping water. dip man water the
 name thing? meaning words baptisme this. he
 baptized, dipped washed, sign becomming new man,
 loyall subject god, whose person represented old
 time moses, high priests, reigned jews; and
 jesus christ, sonne, god, man, hath redeemed us, and
 shall humane nature represent fathers person eternall
 kingdome resurrection; acknowledge doctrine the

 shall delivered kingdome god, even father,
 shall put rule, authority power")
 manifest, baptisme constitute us another

 life; promise take doctrine apostles direction

forgive, retain sinnes
 
power remission, retention sinnes, called also power
 loosing, binding, sometimes keyes kingdome of
 heaven, consequence authority baptize, refuse to
 baptize. baptisme sacrament allegeance, are
 received kingdome god; say, eternall
 life; say, remission sin: eternall life lost
 committing, recovered remitting mens sins. the
 end baptisme remission sins: therefore st. peter, they
 converted sermon day pentecost, asked what
 doe, advised "repent, baptized name
 jesus, remission sins." therefore seeing baptize
 declare reception men gods kingdome; refuse to
 baptize declare exclusion; followeth, power
 declare cast out, retained it, given same
 apostles, substitutes, successors. therefore our
 saviour breathed upon them, saying, (john 20.22.) "receive holy
 ghost," hee addeth next verse, "whose soever sins ye remit,
 remitted unto them; whose soever sins ye retain, are
 retained." words, granted authority forgive, or
 retain sins, simply absolutely, god forgiveth retaineth them,
 knoweth heart man, truth penitence conversion;
 conditionally, penitent: forgivenesse, or
 absolution, case absolved feigned repentance, is
 thereby without act, sentence absolvent, made void,
 hath effect salvation, contrary, the
 aggravation sin. therefore apostles, successors,
 follow outward marks repentance; appearing, they
 authority deny absolution; appeare not, have
 authority absolve. also observed baptisme:
 converted jew, gentile, apostles power to
 deny baptisme; grant un-penitent. seeing man is
 able discern truth another mans repentance, by
 externall marks, taken words, actions, subject to
 hypocrisie; another question will arise, constituted
 judge marks. question decided saviour
 himself; (mat. 18. 15, 16, 17.) "if thy brother (saith he) shall
 trespasse thee, go tell fault thee, him
 alone; shall hear thee, thou hast gained thy brother. he
 will hear thee, take thee one, two more. he
 shall neglect hear them, tell unto church, let unto
 thee heathen man, publican." manifest, that
 judgment concerning truth repentance, belonged one
 man, church, is, assembly faithfull, or
 authority bee representant. besides the
 judgment, necessary also pronouncing sentence: and
 belonged alwaies apostle, pastor church,
 prolocutor; saviour speaketh 18 verse,
 "whatsoever ye shall bind earth, shall bound heaven; and
 whatsoever ye shall loose earth, shall loosed heaven." and
 comformable hereunto practise st. paul (1 cor. 5.3, 4, & 5.)
 saith, "for verily, absent body, present spirit,
 determined already, though present, concerning that
 hath done deed; name lord jesus christ ye
 gathered together, spirit, power lord jesus
 christ, deliver one satan;" say, cast him
 church, man whose sins forgiven. paul here
 pronounceth sentence; assembly first hear cause,
 (for st. paul absent;) consequence condemn him. in
 chapter (ver. 11, 12.) judgment case more
 expressely attributed assembly: "but now written unto

fault lyeth excommunication
 
lyeth excommunication injustice; (mat. 18.) thy brother

 church; obey not, "let thee heathen
 man, publican." lyeth excommunication scandalous

 appeareth authority scripture, example the

 member church, teacheth neverthelesse private opinion, which
 church forbidden: one, s. paul adviseth titus, after

persons liable excommunication

 one voice, one church; part

power make scripture law
 
two senses, wherein writing may said canonicall;
 canon, signifieth rule; rule precept, man
 guided, directed action whatsoever. precepts, though
 given teacher disciple, counsellor friend,
 without power compell observe them, neverthelesse canons;
 rules: given one, that
 receiveth bound obey, canons, onely rules,
 laws: question therefore here, power make the
 scriptures (which rules christian faith) laws.
 



ten commandements
 
part scripture, first law, ten
 commandements, written two tables stone, delivered god
 himselfe moses; moses made known people. that
 time written law god, yet chosen any
 people bee peculiar kingdome, given law men, the
 law nature, say, precepts naturall reason, written
 every mans heart. two tables, first containeth the
 law soveraignty; 1. obey, honour gods of
 nations, words, "non habebis deos alienos coram me," that
 is, "thou shalt gods, gods nations worship;
 onely me:" whereby forbidden obey, honor, their
 king governour, god, spake unto by
 moses, afterwards high priest. 2. "should make
 image represent him;" say, choose to
 themselves, neither heaven, earth, representative their
 fancying, obey moses aaron, appointed that
 office. 3. "they take name god vain;" is,
 speak rashly king, dispute right,
 commissions moses aaron, lieutenants. 4. "they
 every seventh day abstain ordinary labour," employ
 time publique honor. second table containeth the
 duty one man towards another, "to honor parents; kill;
 commit adultery; steale; corrupt judgment false
 witnesse;" finally, "not much designe heart the
 injury one another." question now is, was
 gave written tables obligatory force lawes. there
 doubt made laws god himselfe: a
 law obliges not, law any, acknowledge to
 act soveraign, people israel were
 forbidden approach mountain hear god said moses, be
 obliged obedience laws moses propounded them?
 indeed laws nature, second table;
 therefore acknowledged gods laws; israelites
 alone, people: peculiar the
 israelites, first table, question remains; saving
 obliged themselves, presently propounding of
 them, obey moses, words (exod. 20.19.) "speak thou to
 us, will hear thee; let god speak us, lest die." it
 therefore onely moses then, high priest, (by
 moses) god declared administer peculiar kingdome, that
 earth, power make short scripture decalogue
 bee law common-wealth israel. moses, aaron, the
 succeeding high priests civill soveraigns. therefore hitherto,
 canonizing, making scripture law, belonged civill
 soveraigne.

 man man; leviticall law, say, rule

 whether laws written, written, dictated to
 people moses (after forty dayes god mount)
 word mouth, expressed text; all

 moses civill soveraign.

paul barnabas made apostles church antioch
 
never apostle ordained, paul and
 barnabas, done (as read acts 13.1,2,3.) manner.
 "there church antioch, certaine prophets, and

manifest, though called holy ghost,

 antioch, apostles, s. paul declareth plainly (rom. 1.1.)
 hee useth word, holy ghost used calling:

offices church magisteriall
 
bishop, word formed language, greek episcopus,
 signifieth overseer, superintendent businesse, and
 particularly pastor shepherd; thence metaphor taken, not
 amongst jews originally shepherds, also amongst
 heathen, signifie office king, ruler,
 guide people, whether ruled laws, doctrine. so
 apostles first christian bishops, instituted christ
 himselfe: sense apostleship judas called (acts 1.20.)
 bishoprick. afterwards, constituted elders in
 christian churches, charge guide christs flock their
 doctrine, advice; elders also called bishops. timothy was
 elder (which word elder, new testament name office, as
 well age;) yet also bishop. bishops content
 title elders. nay s. john himselfe, apostle beloved of
 lord, beginneth second epistle words, "the elder to
 elect lady." evident, bishop, pastor, elder,
 doctor, say, teacher, many divers names of
 office time apostles. no
 government coercion, doctrine, perswading. the
 kingdome god yet come, new world; could
 authority compell church, till common-wealth
 embraced christian faith; consequently diversity of
 authority, though diversity employments.
 
besides magisteriall employments church, namely apostles,
 bishops, elders, pastors, doctors, whose calling proclaim
 christ jews, infidels, direct, teach that
 beleeved read new testament other. names
 evangelists prophets, signified office, severall
 gifts, severall men profitable church: as
 evangelists, writing life acts saviour; were
 s. matthew s. john apostles, s. marke s. luke disciples, and
 whosoever else wrote subject, (as s. thomas, s. barnabas are
 said done, though church received books
 gone names:) prophets, gift of
 interpreting old testament; sometimes declaring their
 speciall revelations church. neither gifts, the
 gifts languages, gift casting devils, curing
 diseases, thing else make officer church,
 save onely due calling election charge teaching.

apostles, matthias, paul, barnabas, made our

first book
 
five books hath written subject, first containeth
 three questions: one, simply best government, monarchy,
 aristocracy, democracy; concludeth neither, a
 government mixt there: another, best
 government church; concludeth mixt, should
 participate monarchy: third, whether mixt monarchy,
 st. peter place monarch. concerning first conclusion, i
 already sufficiently proved (chapt. 18.) governments which
 men bound obey, simple, absolute. monarchy is
 one man supreme; men kind power in
 state, commission, pleasure; execute
 name: aristocracy, democracy, one supreme
 assembly, power monarchy belongeth monarch,
 mixt, absolute soveraignty. three
 sorts, best, disputed, one them
 already established; present alwaies preferred,
 maintained, accounted best; law of
 nature, divine positive law, doe thing tending the
 subversion thereof. besides, maketh nothing power of
 pastor, (unlesse civill soveraignty,) kind of
 government best; calling govern men by

 leave consider, whether shall embrace, reject the
 doctrine taught. monarchy, aristocracy, democracy, mark out
 unto us three sorts soveraigns, pastors; or, may say,
 three sorts masters families, three sorts schoolmasters for
 children.
 
therefore second conclusion, concerning best form of
 government church, nothing question popes power
 without dominions: common-wealths power (if
 hee all) schoolmaster onely, the
 master family.
 
third conclusion, is, st. peter monarch the
 church, bringeth chiefe argument place s. matth.
 (chap. 16.18, 19.) "thou art peter, upon rock will build my
 church, &c. will give thee keyes heaven; whatsoever thou

 proveth more, church christ hath foundation one
 onely article; namely, peter name apostles
 professing, gave occasion saviour speak words cited;
 wee may cleerly understand, consider, our
 saviour preached himself, john baptist, apostles,
 nothing article faith, "that christ;" other
 articles requiring faith otherwise, founded that. john
 began first, (mat. 3.2.) preaching this, "the kingdome god at
 hand." saviour (mat. 4.17.) preached same: to
 twelve apostles, gave commission (mat. 10.7.)
 mention preaching article that. was
 fundamentall article, foundation churches faith.
 afterwards apostles returned him, asketh all, (mat.

 "some said john baptist, elias, others jeremias,
 one prophets:" (ver. 15.) asked again, (not
 peter onely) "whom say yee am?" therefore peter answered (for
 all) "thou art christ, living god;" said is
 foundation faith whole church; saviour
 takes occasion saying, "upon stone will build church;"
 manifest, foundation-stone church, was
 meant fundamentall article churches faith. (will
 object) doth saviour interpose words, "thou art peter"?
 originall text rigidly translated, reason
 easily appeared: therefore consider, the
 apostle simon, surnamed stone, (which signification of
 syriacke word cephas, greek word petrus). saviour
 therefore confession fundamentall article, alluding

 upon stone will build church: much say, this
 article, "i christ," foundation faith i
 require bee members church: neither this
 allusion name, unusuall thing common speech: been
 strange, obscure speech, saviour intending build his
 church person st. peter, said, "thou art stone, and
 upon stone will build church," obvious without
 ambiguity said, "i will build church thee; yet there
 still allusion name.
 
following words, "i will give thee keyes heaven, &c."
 saviour gave also rest his
 disciples (matth. 18.18.) "whatsoever yee shall bind earth, shall be
 bound heaven. whatsoever ye shall loose earth, shall loosed
 heaven." howsoever interpreted, doubt but
 power granted belongs supreme pastors; all
 christian civill soveraignes dominions. much, if
 st. peter, saviour converted beleeve
 him, acknowledge kingdome; yet kingdome of

 antichrist yet come; whereas, many popes come gone.
 true, pope taking upon give laws christian
 kings, nations, usurpeth kingdome world, christ took

fourth book
 
fourth book, prove pope supreme judg all
 questions faith manners, (which much absolute
 monarch christians world,) bringeth three propositions:
 first, judgments infallible: second, can
 make laws, punish observe not: third, that
 saviour conferred jurisdiction ecclesiasticall pope of
 rome.

texts point manners
 
infallibility judgment concerning manners, hee bringeth

 following. place say more, though granted,
 pope possibly teach error all, yet doth this

 unlesse shall also say, man obliged conscience set on

 formerly promised work another.

 lawfull soveraign.

 himselfe, civill soveraign christians the

 many precepts saviour apostles, delivered us the

popes temporall power
 
fift book hath four conclusions. first is, "that pope
 lord world:" second, "that pope lord
 christian world:" third, "that pope (without owne
 territory) temporall jurisdiction directly:" three
 conclusions easily granted. fourth is, "that pope (in
 dominions princes) supreme temporall power indirectly:"
 denyed; unlesse mean indirectly, gotten by
 indirect means; also granted. understand, that
 saith hath indirectly, means, temporall
 jurisdiction belongeth right, right a
 consequence pastorall authority, exercise,
 unlesse it: therefore pastorall power
 (which calls spirituall) supreme power civill necessarily
 annexed; thereby hee hath right change kingdomes, giving
 one, taking another, shall think it
 conduces salvation souls.
 
come consider arguments hee prove this
 doctrine, will bee amisse lay open consequences it;
 princes, states, civill soveraignty their
 severall common-wealths, may bethink themselves, whether bee
 convenient them, conducing good subjects, of
 give account day judgment, admit the
 same.
 
said, pope hath (in territories states)
 supreme civill power directly; understand, doth
 challenge it, civill soveraigns doe, originall
 submission thereto governed. evident,
 already sufficiently treatise demonstrated, that
 right soveraigns, derived originally consent of
 every one bee governed; whether choose
 him, doe common defence enemy, they
 agree amongst appoint man, assembly men to
 protect them; whether doe it, save lives, submission
 conquering enemy. pope therefore, disclaimeth the
 supreme civill power states directly, denyeth more, but
 right cometh way; ceaseth that,
 claime another way; is, (without consent them
 governed) right given god, (which hee calleth
 indirectly,) assumption papacy. way soever he
 pretend, power same; may (if bee granted his
 right) depose princes states, often salvation
 soules, is, often will; claimeth also sole
 power judge, whether salvation mens souls, not.
 doctrine, onely bellarmine here, many other
 doctors teach sermons books, also some
 councells decreed, popes decreed, popes have
 accordingly, occasion hath served them, put practise. for
 fourth councell lateran held pope innocent third, (in
 third chap. haereticis,) hath canon. "if king the
 popes admonition, doe purge kingdome haeretiques, being
 excommunicate same, make satisfaction within year, his
 subjects absolved obedience." practise hereof hath
 seen divers occasions; deposing chilperique, king
 france; translation roman empire charlemaine; in
 oppression john king england; transferring kingdome
 navarre; late years, league henry third of
 france, many occurrences. think princes that
 consider injust, inconvenient; wish would
 resolve kings, subjects. men serve two masters: they
 therefore ease them, either holding reins government
 wholly hands; wholly delivering the
 hands pope; men willing obedient, may be
 protected obedience. distinction temporall, and
 spirituall power words. power really divided, as
 dangerously purposes, sharing another indirect power, as
 direct one. come now arguments.
 
first this, "the civill power subject spirituall:
 therefore hath supreme power spirituall, hath right to
 command temporall princes, dispose temporalls order to
 spirituall. distinction temporall, spirituall,
 let us consider sense may said intelligibly, the
 temporall, civill power subject spirituall. but
 two ways words can made sense. wee say, one power
 subject another power, meaning either is, hath
 one, subject hath other; one power is
 other, means end. wee understand, that
 one power hath power another power; one power can have
 right command another: subjection, command, right, and
 power accidents, powers, persons: one power may be
 subordinate another, art sadler, art rider.
 granted, civill government ordained means
 bring us spirituall felicity; yet follow, a
 king civill power, pope spirituall, therefore
 king bound obey pope, every sadler bound to
 obey every rider. therefore subordination art, be
 inferred subjection professor; subordination of
 government, inferred subjection governor. when
 therefore saith, civill power subject spirituall, his
 meaning is, civill soveraign, subject spirituall
 soveraign. argument stands thus, "the civil soveraign, is
 subject spirituall; therefore spirituall prince may
 command temporall princes." conclusion same, the
 antecedent proved. prove it, alledgeth
 first, reason, "kings popes, clergy laity make one
 common-wealth; say, one church: bodies the
 members depend one upon another: things spirituall depend not
 things temporall: therefore, temporall depend spirituall. and
 therefore subject them." argumentation two
 grosse errours: one is, christian kings, popes, clergy, all
 christian men, make one common-wealth: evident that
 france one common-wealth, spain another, venice third, &c. and
 consist christians; therefore also severall bodies
 christians; say, severall churches: severall
 soveraigns represent them, whereby capable commanding and
 obeying, suffering, natural man; generall or
 universall church is, till representant; hath on
 earth: had, doubt christendome were
 one common-wealth, whose soveraign representant, in
 things spirituall temporall: pope, make this
 representant, wanteth three things saviour hath given
 him, command, judge, punish, otherwise (by
 excommunication) run will learn him: for
 though pope christs onely vicar, yet exercise his
 government, till saviours second coming: also the
 pope, st. peter himselfe, apostles, be
 judges world.
 
errour first argument is, sayes, the
 members every common-wealth, naturall body, depend one of
 another: true, cohaere together; depend onely the
 soveraign, soul common-wealth; failing, the
 common-wealth dissolved civill war, one man much
 cohaering another, want common dependance known
 soveraign; just members naturall body dissolve earth,
 want soul hold together. therefore nothing in
 similitude, whence inferre dependance laity the
 clergy, temporall officers spirituall; on
 civill soveraign; indeed direct civill commands
 salvation souls; therefore subject god
 himselfe. thus see laboured fallacy first argument,
 deceive men distinguish subordination of
 actions way end; subjection persons one to
 another administration means. every end, means
 determined nature, god himselfe supernaturally: the
 power make men use means, every nation resigned (by the
 law nature, forbiddeth men violate faith given) the
 civill soveraign.
 
second argument this, "every common-wealth, (because is
 supposed perfect sufficient self,) may command any
 common-wealth, subject it, force change the
 administration government, nay depose prince, set another
 room, otherwise defend selfe injuries
 goes doe them: much may spirituall common-wealth
 command temporall one change administration their
 government, may depose princes, institute others, they
 otherwise defend spirituall good."
 
common-wealth, defend selfe injuries, may lawfully
 doe hath said, true; hath already that
 hath gone sufficiently demonstrated. were
 also true, now world spirituall common-wealth,
 distinct civill common-wealth, might prince thereof,
 upon injury done him, upon want caution injury done
 time come, repaire, secure warre; in
 summe, deposing, killing, subduing, act hostility.
 reason, lesse lawfull civill
 soveraign, upon like injuries done, feared, make warre
 upon spirituall soveraign; beleeve cardinall
 bellarmine inferred proposition.
 
spirituall common-wealth none world: the
 thing kingdome christ; himselfe saith, not
 world; shall next world, resurrection, when
 lived justly, beleeved christ, shall
 (though died naturall bodies) rise spirituall bodies; it
 is, saviour shall judge world, conquer adversaries,
 make spirituall common-wealth. mean time, seeing are
 men earth, whose bodies spirituall; can spirituall
 common-wealth amongst men yet flesh; unlesse wee call
 preachers, commission teach, prepare men for
 reception kingdome christ resurrection, a
 common-wealth; proved bee none.
 
third argument this; "it lawfull christians to
 tolerate infidel, haereticall king, case endeavour draw
 haeresie, infidelity. judge whether king draw
 subjects haeresie, not, belongeth pope. therefore hath
 pope right, determine whether prince deposed, not
 deposed."
 
answer, assertions false. christians,
 (or men religion soever,) tolerate king,
 whatsoever law hee maketh, though bee concerning religion, doe
 violate faith, contrary divine law, naturall and
 positive: judge haeresie amongst subjects, but
 civill soveraign; "haeresie nothing else, private
 opinion, obstinately maintained, contrary opinion the
 publique person (that say, representant common-wealth)
 hath commanded bee taught." manifest, an
 opinion publiquely appointed bee taught, haeresie; the
 soveraign princes authorize them, haeretiques. haeretiques are
 none private men, stubbornly defend doctrine, prohibited
 lawful soveraigns.
 
prove christians tolerate infidell, or
 haereticall kings, alledgeth place deut. 17. god
 forbiddeth jews, shall set king themselves, to
 choose stranger; thence inferreth, unlawfull for
 christian, choose king, christian. ’tis true,
 christian, is, hee hath already obliged
 receive saviour shall come, king, shal

 already attained unto. hence comes passe, men
 means acknowledge owne darknesse, onely by
 reasoning un-forseen mischances, befall their
 ways; darkest part kingdome satan, is
 without church god; say, amongst beleeve not
 jesus christ. say, therefore church enjoyeth
 (as land goshen) light, performance of
 work enjoined us god, necessary. whence comes it, in
 christendome been, almost time apostles,
 justling one another places, forraign,
 civill war? stumbling every little asperity own
 fortune, every little eminence men? such
 diversity ways running mark, felicity, not
 night amongst us, least mist? wee therefore yet dark.
 



four causes spirituall darknesse
 
enemy night naturall ignorance, sown
 tares spirituall errors; that, first, abusing, and
 putting light scriptures: erre, knowing the
 scriptures. secondly, introducing daemonology heathen
 poets, say, fabulous doctrine concerning daemons, which
 idols, phantasms braine, without reall nature of
 own, distinct humane fancy; dead mens ghosts, and
 fairies, matter old wives tales. thirdly, mixing with
 scripture divers reliques religion, much vain and
 erroneous philosophy greeks, especially aristotle. fourthly,
 mingling these, false, uncertain traditions, and
 fained, uncertain history. come erre, "giving heed
 seducing spirits," daemonology "as speak lies in
 hypocrisie," (or originall, 1 tim. 4.1,2. "of that
 play part lyars") "with seared conscience," is, contrary
 knowledge. concerning first these, the
 seducing men abuse scripture, intend speak briefly this
 chapter.

pastors clergy
 
opinion, present church kingdome god,
 proceeds pastours, deacons, ministers the
 church, take name clergy, giving other
 christians name laity, is, simply people. clergy
 signifies those, whose maintenance revenue, god having
 reserved himselfe reigne israelites, assigned
 tribe levi (who publique ministers, no
 portion land set live on, brethren) their
 inheritance. pope therefore, (pretending present church be,
 realme israel, kingdome god) challenging himselfe
 subordinate ministers, like revenue, inheritance of
 god, name clergy sutable claime. thence is,
 tithes, tributes paid levites, gods right,
 amongst israelites, long time demanded, taken of
 christians, ecclesiastiques, jure divino, is, gods right. by
 meanes, people every obliged double tribute;
 one state, another clergy; whereof, clergy,
 tenth revenue, double king of
 athens (and esteemed tyrant) exacted subjects defraying
 publique charges: demanded twentieth part;
 yet abundantly maintained therewith commonwealth. the
 kingdome jewes, sacerdotall reigne god, tithes
 offerings whole publique revenue.
 
mistaking present church kingdom god,

 changed, consecration, either extraordinary worke of

 pretending change nature consecrations,) cannot
 esteemed work extraordinary, conjuration or

 turned rods serpents, water bloud, are
 thought deluded senses spectators false shew
 things, yet esteemed enchanters: wee thought

 water, faced king, serpents
 looked like rods, bloud seemed water? that
 enchantment, lying. yet daily act of
 priest, doe same, turning holy words the
 manner charme, produceth nothing now sense; they
 face us down, hath turned bread man; nay more, into
 god; require men worship it, saviour himself
 present god man, thereby commit grosse idolatry. if
 bee enough excuse idolatry, say bread, but
 god; excuse serve egyptians, case they
 faces say, leeks, onyons worshipped, were
 leeks, onyons, divinity species, or
 likenesse. words, "this body," aequivalent these,

 sacrifice peace-offering, house dedicated. no

 asperges me, impertinent application words spoken upon

answer texts alledged purgatory
 
upon doctrine naturall eternity separated soules, is
 founded (as said) doctrine purgatory. supposing eternall
 life grace onely, life, life body; no
 immortality till resurrection. texts purgatory alledged by
 bellarmine canonicall scripture old testament, are
 first, fasting david saul jonathan, mentioned (2 kings,
 1. 12.); againe, (2 sam. 3. 35.) death abner. this
 fasting david, saith, obtaining something them
 gods hands, death; fasted procure
 recovery owne child, assoone know dead, he
 called meate. seeing soule hath existence separate from
 body, nothing can obtained mens fasting soules
 already either heaven, hell, followeth be
 soules dead men, neither heaven, hell; and
 therefore must bee third place, must purgatory.
 thus hard straining, hee wrested places proofe
 purgatory; whereas manifest, ceremonies mourning,
 fasting, used death men, whose life was
 profitable mourners, used honours sake their
 persons; tis done death whose life the
 mourners benefit, proceeds particular dammage: so
 david honoured saul, abner, fasting; death of
 owne child, recomforted himselfe, receiving ordinary food.
 
places, alledgeth old testament, there
 much shew, colour proofe. brings every text
 wherein word anger, fire, burning, purging, or
 clensing, case fathers sermon rhetorically
 applied doctrine purgatory, already beleeved. first
 verse psalme, 37. "o lord rebuke thy wrath, chasten me
 thy hot displeasure:" purgatory, augustine had
 applied wrath fire hell, displeasure, that
 purgatory? purgatory, psalme, 66. 12. "wee
 went fire water, thou broughtest us moist place;"
 like texts, (with doctors times
 entended adorne, extend sermons, commentaries) haled to
 purposes force wit?
 



places new testament purgatory answered
 
alledgeth places new testament, not
 easie answered: first matth. 12.32. "whosoever
 speaketh word sonne man, shall forgiven him; but
 whosoever speaketh holy ghost, shall bee forgiven
 neither world, world come:" will have
 purgatory world come, wherein sinnes may forgiven,
 world forgiven: notwithstanding is
 manifest, three worlds; one creation the
 flood, destroyed water, called scripture the
 old world; another flood day judgement, the
 present world, shall bee destroyed fire; third, which

chapter xlv. daemonology, reliques religion the
 gentiles
 



originall daemonology
 
impression made organs sight, lucide bodies, either in
 one direct line, many lines, reflected opaque, refracted
 passage diaphanous bodies, produceth living creatures,
 god hath placed organs, imagination object, from
 whence impression proceedeth; imagination called sight; and
 seemeth bee meer imagination, body selfe without
 us; manner, man violently presseth eye, there
 appears light without, him, man perceiveth
 himselfe; indeed thing without him, but
 onely motion interiour organs, pressing resistance
 outward, makes think so. motion made pressure,
 continuing object caused removed, call
 imagination, memory, (in sleep, sometimes great distemper
 organs sicknesse, violence) dream: things have
 already spoken briefly, second third chapters.
 
nature sight never discovered ancient
 pretenders naturall knowledge; much lesse consider not
 things remote (as knowledge is) present use; was
 hard men conceive images fancy, sense,
 otherwise, things really without us: (because they
 vanish away, know whither, how,) will absolutely
 incorporeall, say immateriall, formes without matter;
 colour figure, without coloured figured body; they
 can put aiery bodies (as garment) make visible when
 will bodily eyes; others say, bodies, living
 creatures, made air, subtile aethereall matter,
 is, then, will seen, condensed. them
 agree one generall appellation them, daemons. dead of
 dreamed, inhabitants brain, the
 air, heaven, hell; phantasmes, ghosts; just
 much reason, one say, saw ghost a
 looking-glasse, ghosts stars river; call the
 ordinary apparition sun, quantity foot, the
 daemon, ghost great sun enlighteneth whole visible
 world: means feared them, things unknown, that
 is, unlimited power doe good, harme; consequently,
 given occasion governours heathen common-wealths to
 regulate fear, establishing daemonology (in which
 poets, principal priests heathen religion, specially
 employed, reverenced) publique peace, obedience of
 subjects necessary thereunto; make good daemons,
 others evill; one spurre observance, other, as
 reines withhold violation laws.
 



daemons ancients
 
kind things were, attributed name of
 daemons, appeareth partly genealogie gods, written by
 hesiod, one ancient poets graecians; partly in

 chapter discourse.
 



doctrine spread
 
graecians, colonies conquests, communicated their
 language writings asia, egypt, italy; therein, by
 necessary consequence daemonology, (as st. paul calles it)
 "their doctrines devils;" meanes, contagion was
 derived also jewes, judaea, alexandria, other
 parts, whereinto dispersed. name daemon did
 (as graecians) attribute spirits good, evill; but
 evill onely: good daemons gave name the
 spirit god; esteemed whose bodies entred be
 prophets. summe, singularity good, attributed the
 spirit god; evill, daemon, kakodaimen, evill
 daemon, is, devill. therefore, called daemoniaques, that
 is, possessed devill, call madmen lunatiques; or
 falling sicknesse; spoke thing, they
 want understanding, thought absurd: also unclean person

 see death aeternum, (john 8. 52.) "now know thou hast devill;

 hast devill, goeth kill thee?" whereby manifest,
 jewes opinions concerning phantasmes, namely, that
 phantasmes is, idols braine, things reall,
 independent fancy.

 difficult understand. air many things

 therefore spirits, neither bodies, meer

 hear: command god, light, the

worship exhibite esteem men, kings,

 wee serve him: kinds service contained, onely

chapter xlvi. darknesse vain philosophy, fabulous traditions
 



philosophy is
 
philosophy understood "the knowledge acquired reasoning, from
 manner generation thing, properties; from
 properties, possible way generation same; the
 end bee able produce, far matter, humane force permit,
 effects, humane life requireth." geometrician, the
 construction figures, findeth many properties thereof; from
 properties, new ways construction, reasoning; end
 able measure land water; infinite uses. so
 astronomer, rising, setting, moving sun, and
 starres, divers parts heavens, findeth causes day,
 night, different seasons year; whereby keepeth
 account time: like sciences.
 



prudence part philosophy
 
definition evident, account any
 part thereof, originall knowledge called experience, which
 consisteth prudence: attained reasoning, found
 well brute beasts, man; memory successions
 events times past, wherein omission every little
 circumstance altering effect, frustrateth expectation the
 prudent: whereas nothing produced reasoning aright, but
 generall, eternall, immutable truth.
 



false doctrine part philosophy
 
therefore give name false conclusions: he

 error:

man knows supernaturall revelation; it

men, law governs

review, conclusion
 

contrariety naturall faculties mind, one
 another, also one passion another, reference
 conversation, argument taken, inferre an
 impossibility one man sufficiently disposed all
 sorts civill duty. severity judgment, say, makes men
 censorious, unapt pardon errours infirmities other
 men: side, celerity fancy, makes thoughts lesse
 steddy necessary, discern exactly right wrong.
 again, deliberations, pleadings, faculty solid
 reasoning, necessary: without it, resolutions men are
 rash, sentences unjust: yet powerfull
 eloquence, procureth attention consent, effect reason
 will little. contrary faculties; former being
 grounded upon principles truth; upon opinions already
 received, true, false; upon passions interests men,
 different, mutable.
 
amongst passions, courage, (by mean contempt of
 wounds, violent death) enclineth men private revenges, and
 sometimes endeavour unsetling publique peace; and
 timorousnesse, many times disposeth desertion publique
 defence. say stand together person.
 
consider contrariety mens opinions, manners in
 generall, say, impossible entertain constant civill
 amity those, businesse world constrains
 us converse: businesse consisteth almost nothing else a
 perpetuall contention honor, riches, authority.
 
answer, indeed great difficulties, not
 impossibilities: education, discipline, may bee, and
 sometimes reconciled. judgment, fancy may place the
 man; turnes; end aimeth requireth. the
 israelites egypt, sometimes fastened labour making
 bricks, times ranging abroad gather straw: also may
 judgment sometimes fixed upon one certain consideration, and
 fancy another time wandring world. also reason,
 eloquence, (though perhaps naturall sciences, yet the
 morall) may stand well together. wheresoever place for
 adorning preferring errour, much place adorning
 preferring truth, adorn. any
 repugnancy fearing laws, fearing publique enemy;
 abstaining injury, pardoning others. is
 therefore inconsistence humane nature, civill duties,
 think. known cleernesse judgment, largenesse of
 fancy; strength reason, gracefull elocution; courage the
 warre, fear laws, eminently one man; that
 noble honored friend mr. sidney godolphin; hating no
 man, hated any, unfortunately slain beginning the
 late civill warre, publique quarrel, indiscerned, an
 undiscerning hand.

 lawfully, hee will. therefore doe it, undoubtedly

also man may understand, is, men may said to
 conquered; nature conquest, right a
